This is inefficient because:\n   - The config loading might be expensive (making HTTP requests to fetch IAM role credentials)\n   - The loaded config is not being reused\n\n3. **No credential refresh strategy**: The implementation relies entirely on the AWS SDK's internal credential caching, which might not refresh credentials in time if they expire.\n\nThe fix should be to:\n1.
